<script>
    StackExchange.ready(function () {
        StackExchange.Hero.init("stk", "a");

        var location = 0;
        if ($("body").hasClass("questions-page")) {
            location = 1;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("question-page")) {
            location = 1;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("faq-page")) {
            location = 5;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("home-page")) {
            location = 3;
        }

        $('.js-cta-button').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("hero.action", { hero_action_type: 'cta', location: location }, true);
            });
        });

        // TODO: we should review the class names and whatnot in use here. Older heroes use id selectors, the newer
        // sticky question hero on SO has a .js-dismiss class instead, but it's apparently not used anywhere... 
        // It's not great. Ideally we'd have a set of classes in the partials above that would correspond to 
        // the behaviours we want here in a more clear way. 

        // sticky question-page hero at the bottom of the page on SO
        $('.js-dismiss').on('click', function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("hero.action", { hero_action_type: "close", location: location }, true);
            });
            StackExchange.Hero.dismiss();
            $(".js-dismissable-hero").fadeOut("fast");
        });
    });
</script>

        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/249937/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<pre><code>/"(?:[^"\\]|\\.)*"/
</code></pre>

<p>Works in The Regex Coach and PCRE Workbench.</p>

<p>Example of test in JavaScript:</p>

<p></p><div class="snippet" data-babel="false" data-console="true" data-hide="false" data-lang="js">
<div class="snippet-code">
<pre class="snippet-code-js lang-js prettyprint-override"><code>    var s = ' function(){ return " Is big \\"problem\\", \\no? "; }';
    var m = s.match(/"(?:[^"\\]|\\.)*"/);
    if (m != null)
        alert(m);</code></pre>
</div>
</div>
<p></p>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>This one comes from nanorc.sample available in many linux distros.  It is used for syntax highlighting of C style strings</p>

<pre><code>\"(\\.|[^\"])*\"
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>As provided by ePharaoh, the answer is</p>

<pre><code>/"([^"\\]*(\\.[^"\\]*)*)"/
</code></pre>

<p>To have the above apply to either single quoted or double quoted strings, use</p>

<pre><code>/"([^"\\]*(\\.[^"\\]*)*)"|\'([^\'\\]*(\\.[^\'\\]*)*)\'/
</code></pre>
    </div>

<div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="30737232" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="249791" data-position-on-page="4" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="12" id="answer-30737232" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">

        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="30737232">
        <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z"></path></svg>
        </button>
        <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="12" itemprop="upvoteCount">
            12
        </div>
        <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z"></path></svg>
        </button>



            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
                <div class="ta-center">
                    <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z"></path></svg>
                </div>
            </div>

    
        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/30737232/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Most of the solutions provided here use alternative repetition paths i.e. (A|B)*.</p>

<p>You may encounter stack overflows on large inputs since some pattern compiler implements this using recursion.</p>

<p>Java for instance: <a href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/bugs.java.com/bugdatabase/view_bug.do?bug_id=6337993" rel="noreferrer">http://bugs.java.com/bugdatabase/view_bug.do?bug_id=6337993</a></p>

<p>Something like this:
<code>"(?:[^"\\]*(?:\\.)?)*"</code>, or the one provided by Guy Bedford will reduce the amount of parsing steps avoiding most stack overflows.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

    <div class="post-layout">

        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/249804/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<pre><code>/(["\']).*?(?&lt;!\\)(\\\\)*\1/is
</code></pre>

<p>should work with any quoted string</p>
    </div>

<div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="4448207" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="249791" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="9" id="answer-4448207" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="4448207">

        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/4448207/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<pre><code>"(?:\\"|.)*?"
</code></pre>

<p>Alternating the <code>\"</code> and the <code>.</code> passes over escaped quotes while the lazy quantifier <code>*?</code> ensures that you don't go past the end of the quoted string. Works with .NET Framework RE classes</p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">

            <time datetime="2010-12-15T08:54:58" itemprop="dateCreated"></time>
            <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

<a name="33617839"></a>
<div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="33617839" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="249791" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="8" id="answer-33617839" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="33617839">
        <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z"></path></svg>
        </button>
        <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="8" itemprop="upvoteCount">
            8
        </div>
        <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

        </button>



            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
                <div class="ta-center">
                    <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z"></path></svg>
                </div>
            </div>

    
        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/33617839/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<pre><code>/"(?:[^"\\]++|\\.)*+"/
</code></pre>

<p>Taken straight from <code>man perlre</code> on a Linux system with Perl 5.22.0 installed.
As an optimization, this regex uses the 'posessive' form of both <code>+</code> and <code>*</code> to prevent backtracking, for it is known beforehand that a string without a closing quote wouldn't match in any case.</p>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>This one works perfect on PCRE and does not fall with StackOverflow.</p>

<pre><code>"(.*?[^\\])??((\\\\)+)?+"
</code></pre>

<p>Explanation:</p>

<ol>
<li>Every quoted string starts with Char: <code>"</code> ;</li>
<li>It may contain any number of any characters: <code>.*?</code> {Lazy match}; ending with non escape character <code>[^\\]</code>;</li>
<li>Statement (2) is Lazy(!) optional because string can be empty(""). So: <code>(.*?[^\\])??</code></li>
<li>Finally, every quoted string ends with Char(<code>"</code>), but it can be preceded with even number of escape sign pairs <code>(\\\\)+</code>; and it is Greedy(!) optional: <code>((\\\\)+)?+</code> {Greedy matching}, bacause string can be empty or without ending pairs!</li>
</ol>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
            <time datetime="2017-04-24T20:17:43" itemprop="dateCreated"></time>
            <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

                <span class="comment-copy">It isn't the most efficient pattern of the world, but the idea is interesting. Note that you can shorten it like this: <code>"(.*?[^\\])?(\\\\)*"</code></span>
                
              <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>An option that has not been touched on before is:</p>

<ol>
<li>Reverse the string.</li>
<li>Perform the matching on the reversed string.</li>
<li>Re-reverse the matched strings.</li>
</ol>

<p>This has the added bonus of being able to correctly match escaped open tags.</p>

<p>Lets say you had the following string; <code>String \"this "should" NOT match\" and "this \"should\" match"</code>
Here, <code>\"this "should" NOT match\"</code> should not be matched and <code>"should"</code> should be.
On top of that <code>this \"should\" match</code> should be matched and <code>\"should\"</code> should not.</p>

<p>First an example.
</p>

<pre><code>// The input string.
const myString = 'String \\"this "should" NOT match\\" and "this \\"should\\" match"';

// The RegExp.
const regExp = new RegExp(
    // Match close
    '([\'"])(?!(?:[\\\\]{2})*[\\\\](?![\\\\]))' +
    '((?:' +
        // Match escaped close quote
        '(?:\\1(?=(?:[\\\\]{2})*[\\\\](?![\\\\])))|' +
        // Match everything thats not the close quote
        '(?:(?!\\1).)' +
    '){0,})' +
    // Match open
    '(\\1)(?!(?:[\\\\]{2})*[\\\\](?![\\\\]))',
    'g'
);

// Reverse the matched strings.
matches = myString
    // Reverse the string.
    .split('').reverse().join('')
    // '"hctam "\dluohs"\ siht" dna "\hctam TON "dluohs" siht"\ gnirtS'

    // Match the quoted
    .match(regExp)
    // ['"hctam "\dluohs"\ siht"', '"dluohs"']

    // Reverse the matches
    .map(x =&gt; x.split('').reverse().join(''))
    // ['"this \"should\" match"', '"should"']

    // Re order the matches
    .reverse();
    // ['"should"', '"this \"should\" match"']
</code></pre>

<p>Okay, now to explain the RegExp.
This is the regexp can be easily broken into three pieces. As follows:
</p>

<pre><code># Part 1
(['"])         # Match a closing quotation mark " or '
(?!            # As long as it's not followed by
  (?:[\\]{2})* # A pair of escape characters
  [\\]         # and a single escape
  (?![\\])     # As long as that's not followed by an escape
)
# Part 2
((?:          # Match inside the quotes
(?:           # Match option 1:
  \1          # Match the closing quote
  (?=         # As long as it's followed by
    (?:\\\\)* # A pair of escape characters
    \\        # 
    (?![\\])  # As long as that's not followed by an escape
  )           # and a single escape
)|            # OR
(?:           # Match option 2:
  (?!\1).     # Any character that isn't the closing quote
)
)*)           # Match the group 0 or more times
# Part 3
(\1)           # Match an open quotation mark that is the same as the closing one
(?!            # As long as it's not followed by
  (?:[\\]{2})* # A pair of escape characters
  [\\]         # and a single escape
  (?![\\])     # As long as that's not followed by an escape
)
</code></pre>

<p>This is probably a lot clearer in image form: generated using <a href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/jex.im/regulex/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Jex's Regulex</a></p>

<p><a href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/2230835/34616812-3cc9c220-f231-11e7-948b-2429f1551844.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Image on github (JavaScript Regular Expression Visualizer.)</a>
Sorry, I don't have a high enough reputation to include images, so, it's just a link for now.</p>

<p>Here is a gist of an example function using this concept that's a little more advanced: <a href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/gist.github.com/scagood/bd99371c072d49a4fee29d193252f5fc#file-matchquotes-js" rel="nofollow noreferrer">https://gist.github.com/scagood/bd99371c072d49a4fee29d193252f5fc#file-matchquotes-js</a></p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">

                </div>
            </div>

    
        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/45526948/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>here is one that work with both " and ' and you easily add others at the start.</p>

<pre>("|')(?:\\\1|[^\1])*?\1</pre>

<p>it uses the backreference (\1) match exactley what is in the first group (" or '). </p>

<p><a href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/www.regular-expressions.info/backref.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">http://www.regular-expressions.info/backref.html</a></p>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
            <time datetime="2017-08-05T22:37:22" itemprop="dateCreated"></time>
            <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
                


<div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="45526948">
    <div class="d-flex gs8 s-anchors s-anchors__muted fw-wrap">

            <div class="flex--item">

        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy">this is a very good solution, but <code>[^\1]</code> should be replaced with <code>.</code> because there is no such thing as an anti-back-reference, and it doesn't matter anyways.  the first condition will always match before anything bad could happen.</span>
                
              <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
– <a class="comment-user" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/users/4808079/seph-reed" title="6,843 reputation">Seph Reed</a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><span class="relativetime-clean" title="2017-11-02 06:15:42Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">Nov 2, 2017 at 6:15</span></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    </li>
    <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="95032854" data-comment-owner-id="519360" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-95032854">
        <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
            <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
            <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                
                <span class="comment-copy"><b>@SephReed</b> – replacing <code>[^\1]</code> with <code>.</code> would effectively change this regex to <code>("|').*?\1</code> and then it would match <code>"foo\"</code> in <code>"foo \" bar"</code>. That said, getting <code>[^\1]</code> to actually work is hard. <b>@​mathiashansen</b> – You're better off with the unwieldy and expensive <code>(?!\1).</code> (so the whole regex, with some efficiency cleanup, would be <code>(["'])(?:\\.|(?!\1).)*+\1</code>. The <code>+</code> is optional if your engine doesn't support it.</span>
                
              <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
– <a class="comment-user" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/users/519360/adam-katz" title="12,901 reputation">Adam Katz</a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr"><span class="relativetime-clean" title="2019-01-08 21:31:25Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">Jan 8, 2019 at 21:31</span></span>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>One has to remember that regexps aren't a silver bullet for everything string-y. Some stuff are simpler to do with a cursor and linear, manual, seeking. A <a href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Context-free_language" rel="nofollow noreferrer">CFL</a> would do the trick pretty trivially, but there aren't many CFL implementations (afaik).</p>
    </div>

<div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="20352652" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="249791" data-position-on-page="12" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="0" id="answer-20352652" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="20352652">
        <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z"></path></svg>
        </button>
        <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
            0
        </div>
        <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z"></path></svg>
        </button>



            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
                <div class="ta-center">
                    <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z"></path></svg>
                </div>
            </div>

    
        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/20352652/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>A more extensive version of <a href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/a/10786066/1794894">https://stackoverflow.com/a/10786066/1794894</a></p>

<pre><code>/"([^"\\]{50,}(\\.[^"\\]*)*)"|\'[^\'\\]{50,}(\\.[^\'\\]*)*\'|“[^”\\]{50,}(\\.[^“\\]*)*”/   
</code></pre>

<p>This version also contains</p>

<ol>
<li>Minimum quote length of 50</li>
<li>Extra type of quotes (open <code>“</code> and close <code>”</code>)</li>
</ol>
    </div>

<pre><code>\"((\\\")|[^\\])*\"

<div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="49291272" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="249791" data-position-on-page="14" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="0" data-score="0" id="answer-49291272" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
    <div class="post-layout">
        <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
            <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="49291272">
        <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z"></path></svg>
        </button>
        <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
            0
        </div>
        <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z"></path></svg>
        </button>



            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
                <div class="ta-center">
                    <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewBox="0 0 36 36" width="36"><path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z"></path></svg>
                </div>
            </div>

    
        <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/https/stackoverflow.com/posts/49291272/timeline" title="Show activity on this post."><svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewBox="0 0 19 18" width="19"><path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z"></path></svg></a>

</div>

        </div>

        

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>I faced a similar problem trying to remove quoted strings that may interfere with parsing of some files.</p>

<p>I ended up with a two-step solution that beats any convoluted regex you can come up with:</p>

<pre><code> line = line.replace("\\\"","\'"); // Replace escaped quotes with something easier to handle
 line = line.replaceAll("\"([^\"]*)\"","\"x\""); // Simple is beautiful
</code></pre>

<p>Easier to read and probably more efficient.</p>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>If your IDE is IntelliJ Idea, you can forget all these headaches and store your regex into a String variable and as you copy-paste it inside the double-quote it will automatically change to a regex acceptable format.</p>
<p>example in Java:</p>
<pre><code>String s = "\"en_usa\":[^\\,\\}]+";
</code></pre>
<p>now you can use this variable in your regexp or anywhere.</p>
    </div>

<div class="answercell post-layout--right">
    
    <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
<p>Messed around at <a href="https://translated.turbopages.org/proxy_u/en-ru.ru.108988ca-6319a3b7-adef515b-74722d776562/regexpal.com/" rel="nofollow">regexpal</a> and ended up with this regex: (Don't ask me how it works, I barely understand even tho I wrote it lol)</p>

<pre><code>"(([^"\\]?(\\\\)?)|(\\")+)+"
</code></pre>
    </div>
    <div class="mt24">
        <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
